## <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="866e2-1682">Commenti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="866e2-1682">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="866e2-1683">La classe **MS-DFSR-contentt** fa parte del supporto del servizio di replica file System distribuito (DFS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="866e2-1683">The **ms-DFSR-ContentSet** class is a part of the Distributed File System (DFS) Replication service support.</span></span>
